Cover selectors

::after is a selector that adds something after the item selected
descendant selector  - child, grandchildren et etc, use a space " " 
child selector >  oinly immediate child

Fixed - does not move when you scroll
Relative - sets the position relavtive to its original position in the flow
Absolute - sets position based on top left of screen or the top left of the containing relative div - scollable
Padding - space between border and content
Margin - space around element

$(document).ready(function(){
    $("p").click(function(){
        $(this).hide();
    });
});
